<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Football at the 1986 Asian Games</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><p><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Football_(soccer)" title="Football (soccer)">Football</a></b> at the <b><a href="/wiki/1986_Asian_Games" title="1986 Asian Games">1986 Asian Games</a></b> was held in <a href="/wiki/Seoul" title="Seoul">Seoul</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> from September 20 to October 5, 1986. <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a> boycotted to dispatch the national football team.</p>
<p></p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Semifinals">Semifinals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Football_at_the_1986_Asian_Games&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Semifinals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
